# The Loop Design System — Component Rendered HTML Reference

Generated reference of the rendered HTML for every component preview in the Live Style Guide.
Each component shows the HTML inside `.pattern-preview-content`. Where a component renders part of its UI in a portal (dropdown option lists, opened popovers/popups, date-picker calendars), that markup is included in an extra section.

Total components: 88

---

## Table of Contents

- **Adaptive**: [Columns 2](#columns-2), [Columns 3](#columns-3), [Columns 4](#columns-4), [Columns 5](#columns-5), [Columns 6](#columns-6), [Columns Medium Left](#columns-medium-left), [Columns Medium Right](#columns-medium-right), [Columns Small Left](#columns-small-left), [Columns Small Right](#columns-small-right), [Display On Device](#display-on-device), [Gallery](#gallery), [Master Detail](#master-detail)
- **Content**: [Accordion](#accordion), [Alert](#alert), [Blank Slate](#blank-slate), [Card](#card), [Card Background](#card-background), [Card Item](#card-item), [Card Sectioned](#card-sectioned), [Chat Message](#chat-message), [Flip Content](#flip-content), [Floating Content](#floating-content), [List Item Content](#list-item-content), [Section](#section), [Section Group](#section-group), [Tag](#tag), [Tooltip](#tooltip), [User Avatar](#user-avatar)
- **Interaction**: [Action Sheet](#action-sheet), [Animate](#animate), [Animated Label](#animated-label), [Bottom Sheet](#bottom-sheet), [Carousel](#carousel), [Date Picker](#date-picker), [Dropdown Search](#dropdown-search), [Dropdown Tags](#dropdown-tags), [Floating Actions](#floating-actions), [Input With Icon](#input-with-icon), [Lightbox Image](#lightbox-image), [Month Picker](#month-picker), [Notification](#notification), [Range Slider](#range-slider), [Range Slider Interval](#range-slider-interval), [Scrollable Area](#scrollable-area), [Search](#search), [Sidebar](#sidebar), [Stacked Cards](#stacked-cards), [Video](#video)
- **Navigation**: [Bottom Bar Item](#bottom-bar-item), [Breadcrumbs](#breadcrumbs), [Pagination](#pagination), [Section Index](#section-index), [Submenu](#submenu), [Tabs](#tabs), [Timeline Item](#timeline-item), [Wizard](#wizard)
- **Numbers**: [Badge](#badge), [Counter](#counter), [Icon Badge](#icon-badge), [Progress Bar](#progress-bar), [Progress Circle](#progress-circle), [Rating](#rating)
- **Utilities**: [Align Center](#align-center), [Button Loading](#button-loading), [Center Content](#center-content), [Inline SVG](#inline-svg), [Margin Container](#margin-container), [Mouse Events](#mouse-events), [Separator](#separator), [Swipe Events](#swipe-events), [Touch Events](#touch-events)
- **Widgets**: [Button](#button), [Button Group](#button-group), [Checkbox](#checkbox), [Dropdown](#dropdown), [Feedback Message](#feedback-message), [Form](#form), [Input](#input), [Link](#link), [List](#list), [Popover](#popover), [Popup](#popup), [Radio Group](#radio-group), [Switch](#switch), [Table](#table), [TextArea](#textarea), [Upload](#upload)
- **Advanced**: [Dropdown Server Side](#dropdown-server-side)

```html
    <div data-container="" class="columns columns2  tablet- phone- ">
      <div class="columns-item" id="b4-b1-b2-Column1">
```

```html
          <div data-list="" class="list list-group list-loading OSFillParent" id="b4-b12-EmployeeList" style="position: relative;">
            <script style="display: flex; height: 0px; width: 100%;">

            </script>
          </div>

              <i class="icon fa fa-angle-left fa-2x" aria-hidden="true" data-icon="">
              </i>
            </a>
          </div>
```

# Content

## Accordion

_State: default collapsed state_

### `.pattern-preview-content`

```html
<div class="pattern-preview-content" id="b5-b1-b1-Preview">
  <div data-block="Content.Accordion" class="OSBlockWidget" id="b5-b1-$b6">
    <div class="osui-accordion" name="0.edr0ne514kv" id="b5-b1-b6-Content">
      <div data-block="Content.AccordionItem" class="OSBlockWidget" id="b5-b1-$b7">
        <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item osui-accordion-item--is-open" name="0.urppxa7m6x9" id="b5-b1-b7-AccordionItem" aria-disabled="false">
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__title osui-accordion-item__title--is-right osui-accordion-item__click_zone" id="b5-b1-b7-TitleWrapper" default-tabindex-element="" tabindex="0" aria-controls="b5-b1-b7-Content" aria-disabled="false" role="button" aria-expanded="true">
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__title__placeholder" id="b5-b1-b7-Title">I noticed some erratic behavior from my screen</div>
            <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__icon osui-accordion-item__icon--caret" aria-hidden="true" inert="">
            </div>
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__icon placeholder-empty osui-accordion-item__icon--hidden" id="b5-b1-b7-CustomIcon">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__content osui-accordion-item__content--is-expanded" id="b5-b1-b7-ContentWrapper" aria-labelledby="b5-b1-b7-TitleWrapper" role="region" aria-hidden="false">
            <div id="b5-b1-b7-Content">Screens are great assets for anyone working in an office set up. They allow you to have more programs open, multitask and be more productive. Hopefully</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div data-block="Content.AccordionItem" class="OSBlockWidget" id="b5-b1-$b8">
        <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item osui-accordion-item--is-closed" name="0.t5nedt0i7q" id="b5-b1-b8-AccordionItem" aria-disabled="false">
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__title osui-accordion-item__title--is-right osui-accordion-item__click_zone" id="b5-b1-b8-TitleWrapper" default-tabindex-element="" tabindex="0" aria-controls="b5-b1-b8-Content" aria-disabled="false" role="button" aria-expanded="false">
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__title__placeholder" id="b5-b1-b8-Title">Some of my keyboard keys are not working properly</div>
            <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__icon osui-accordion-item__icon--caret" aria-hidden="true" inert="">
            </div>
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__icon placeholder-empty osui-accordion-item__icon--hidden" id="b5-b1-b8-CustomIcon">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__content osui-accordion-item__content--is-collapsed" id="b5-b1-b8-ContentWrapper" aria-labelledby="b5-b1-b8-TitleWrapper" role="region" aria-hidden="true">
            <div id="b5-b1-b8-Content">After a while, it’s common for keyboards to start malfunctioning. We have the habit of pressing the same keys which causes stress on their mechanics leading to problems.</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div data-block="Content.AccordionItem" class="OSBlockWidget" id="b5-b1-$b9">
        <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item osui-accordion-item--is-closed" name="0.ffue7brtm4c" id="b5-b1-b9-AccordionItem" aria-disabled="false">
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__title osui-accordion-item__title--is-right osui-accordion-item__click_zone" id="b5-b1-b9-TitleWrapper" default-tabindex-element="" tabindex="0" aria-controls="b5-b1-b9-Content" aria-disabled="false" role="button" aria-expanded="false">
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__title__placeholder" id="b5-b1-b9-Title">I need a new mouse, the left-click is not working</div>
            <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__icon osui-accordion-item__icon--caret" aria-hidden="true" inert="">
            </div>
            <div class="osui-accordion-item__icon placeholder-empty osui-accordion-item__icon--hidden" id="b5-b1-b9-CustomIcon">
            </div>
          </div>
          <div data-container="" class="osui-accordion-item__content osui-accordion-item__content--is-collapsed" id="b5-b1-b9-ContentWrapper" aria-labelledby="b5-b1-b9-TitleWrapper" role="region" aria-hidden="true">
            <div id="b5-b1-b9-Content">Mice are incredible accelerators that ease navigation and access. They easily become overused, with all the clicking, dragging and scrolling, which means their life can be short.</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
```
